<user_name>M W</user_name>< Review>
The Master Gardener demonstration gardens are spectacular! They have a moon garden, a pollinator friendly habitat (to encourage bees, butterflies, and other beneficial insects to come), and Mediterranean garden with plants from Australia, South Africa, and other countries with similar "western facing" coastal climates (wet winter months followed by dry summer/ fall months). Plus the most fascinating and enormous succulents (check out the agave and aloe plants that have 15ft+ spire-like blooms!). Beautiful building and great place to wander around on a lazy day.< /Review>

Roger K Ng (RKNG)<//name>
<Date>1525145299084< /Date><Rating>4<//Rating>< review>
This place is nicely decor and clean.  This is very important especially when serving raw fishes.  Their poke bowl can be highly customize with quite a few different ingredients.  The fish selection is decent and they are fresh.  The yellow tuna, however, has a surcharge of $1.00 which in my opinion is not worth it due to the small scope they were given me.  The staffs were friendly.  The price is reasonable for dinner.  However, as for lunch, you might be only few dollars away from an average Japanese restaurant quality Chirashi Bowl.  It has a self serving soda fountain and utensil station.  Specialty drinks such as Thai-Tea, Guava Island juice and Tropical juice are also available.  There are plenty of parking space as well.  Recommended.< /review>

< Review>
Food and flavor had me coming back regularly. Customer service however I find to be very rude. One man in particular the other day with a full beard, when I asked to get fresh yellowtail to avoid being served the last of the remaining two pieces of a pan. He refused, and said that to give me more yellowtail would require him to go cut more.

I think this place is very expensive, but flavorful. If the customer service was as good as the food I wouldn't mind coming back. It was a simple request and to have absolutely no effort on this managers part is a shame. I've told others about this incident and being in the hospitality industry myself, I know better, and this guy should too. Highly unlikely that you don't have pre-cut fish prepped during dinner rush, but maybe he didn't want to walk five feet. Never again.<//Review>

<Rating>5</Rating>< text>
This place is my favorite poke spot. They have a lot of toppings and a good amount of choices of fish. The prices are very reasonable. The staff is always friendly. I always get the large bowl with white rice, garlic soy for the sauce, salmon, yellow tail, and tuna. Then the toppings I get seaweed, double crab, cucumber, edamame and salmonroe. Side note some of my friends get all the 9 sauces mixed together. Also extra crab is 75 cents, avocado is $1 and yellowtail is $1. It's sorta hard to find this place.When you get off the freeway at the IKEA go north towards the foothills and make a left at the 2nd light. It will be the on the right when you enter the parking lot. I've been all over the planet and this is my favorite poke spot...for real. I hope you enjoy it.<//text>

<Rating>3< /Rating><Review>As the name of this restaurant implies, there are other Taqueria El Tapatio restaurants in our area. I strongly recommend avoiding this location and visiting one of their other locations if in the mood for Mexican food. You will receive better customer service overall and the quality of the food will be significantly better.

Because I don't believe in ruling a place out based on one bad food experience, I have tried this place multiple times since it opened at The Annex. Unfortunately, this week I cannot deny that the food here is of poor quality and lacks flavor. The salsas and guacamole provided lacked flavor. The tortillas were stale. Part of the food is microwaved (which I'm not against, most of us use a microwave to reheat food, but it did not make the food better in any way). All food was bland. The aguas frescas were passable. Essentially, there was no passion and pride in the making of the food.

A relative ordered a plate which comes with sides and ordered extra tortillas. When we received our order, there were no sides for his plate or extra tortillas. He waited in line instead of cutting in front of anyone and asked about his missing items. The cook immediately got defensive and claimed we never ordered them. Thankfully, the cashier pulled up the receipt without us asking and showed the cook. It goes without saying the order was reluctantly rectified.

Also, another cook which may also be the location's manager, admitted to having the ingredients to make one of the menu items but just didn't feel like making it. This was not a big deal because we obviously still ordered food, but it serves as another example of the service one may experience.

What allows me to give this place 3 stars instead of 2 is the young lady who was the cashier. She was attentive, prompt, and courteous.</Review>< Pictures>

< Review>
Came here on a whim to have hot soup on a rainy chilly day. Found the best Pho in town, well located in a shopping plaza  but a bit hidden on far end. The list of Menu is plentiful, all healthy options. The fresh spring rolls with peanut sauce was sumptuous and the beef stew Pho was perfect choice for a hungry stomach on a cold rainy day. The prices on the Menu are just right. The restaurant was not busy on an afternoon after 2 p.m but this place gets crowded at lunch time and dinner time. This place is big though and clean. Staffs are friendly and attentive. I would certainly come back to try the other foods on the menu!q< /Review>

<review>This is our new favorite local  Pho spot!

The food. For the appetizer, we ordered the spring rolls. Entrees, we ordered the grilled pork with rice and one over easy egg, a #8 pho bowl, and egg noodle soup with wonton. No complaints! And my 8 year old daughter is hard to please, even with a simple bowl of soup. But she left full and 100% satisfied.

This spot won me over the moment I saw they have hot chili OIL. I don't know why all restaurants can't have this! It is a necessity with all Asian foods lol.

Customer service was good. All the staff seemed really nice. Food came out quick. And the waiter was kind enough to check on us more than enough times to make sure we were ok, which doesn't happen everywhere.

The one thing I did not check out was the bathroom. Will see next time but I hope it's clean!

I am not sure how long this place has been around, but we have not been able to find a good Pho spot near home since we have been living here (10 years). This is our new go-to when we are craving Pho!<//review>< user_id>

The only problem I encountered was the scheduling. I was initially told by a live person that my appointment would be at 7:45 a.m.  Later, I received a recording stating my appointment time as 7:45 a.m. but to arrive at 7:15.  Still later, I received another recording stating that my appointment time was 8:30 a.m but to arrive by 8:00 a.m.

Naturally, I didn't want to be late so I arrived at 7:15 a.m.  After completing the paperwork, I proceeded to wait while another person was taken to an office for processing. Soon, a staff member approached me, asked me what time my appointment was and reassured me that I would be next.  I learned that another patient who was also waiting had also received dual recordings. A staff member apologized for the recording mixup but my appointment was at the later time of 8:30 a.m.

I was not angry but this type of error should not be happening, especially so early in the morning.  This review is intended only to alert staff of the problem. Once my appointment time arrived, I received excellent care with only one hiccup of another wait time between tests.<//Review>
